<tr><td><h3><a href="https://github.com/cqlwsw285/djy/blob/master/gb/19/11/4/n11632432.md#1" target="_blank">令生活充满幸福的蛋糕（二）</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/cqlwsw285/djy/blob/master/gb/19/11/4/n11632432.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="http://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2019/11/edb463d4023a338e702b1c61cbcceb81-4-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>文：李沁一?大纪元
一提起蛋糕，耳边就仿佛响起一段歌声：“我轻轻的尝一口这香浓的诱惑，我喜欢的样子你都有。我轻轻的尝一口你说的爱我，舍不得吃会微笑的糖果。”
